At least a few hundred tanks<sup id="cite_ref-nearly_5.2C000_bombs_dropped_on_ISIL_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nearly_5.2C000_bombs_dropped_on_ISIL-45"><span>[</span>45<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46"><span>[</span>46<span>]</span></a></sup><br /></p>
3 drones<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47"><span>[</span>47<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48"><span>[</span>48<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ISIS_controls_Kobani_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ISIS_controls_Kobani-49"><span>[</span>49<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-ISIL_drone_downed_near_Aleppo_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ISIL_drone_downed_near_Aleppo-50"><span>[</span>50<span>]</span></a></sup></td>
<td style="width:33%;padding-left:0.25em">
<p><b>Free Syrian Army</b>:<br />
Between 45,000 and 60,000 fighters (disputed)<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51"><span>[</span>51<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<hr />
<p><b>Islamic Front&#160;:</b><br />
40,000<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52"><span>[</span>52<span>]</span></a></sup>–70,000<sup id="cite_ref-Front_to_back_53-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Front_to_back-53"><span>[</span>53<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<hr />
<p><b>al-Nusra Front:</b><br />
10,000<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54"><span>[</span>54<span>]</span></a></sup><br />
<b>Ahrar ash-Sham</b>:<br /></p>
10,000-20,000<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55"><span>[</span>55<span>]</span></a></sup></td>

<p>On 30 September 2015, Russia started formal military intervention in the <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Civil_War" title="Syrian Civil War">Syrian Civil War</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-latimes_62-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-latimes-62"><span>[</span>62<span>]</span></a></sup> It has consisted of air strikes by Russia against militant groups opposed to the <a href="/wiki/Council_of_Ministers_(Syria)" title="Council of Ministers (Syria)">Syrian government</a>, including <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda_in_the_Levant" title="Al-Qaeda in the Levant" class="mw-redirect">al-Nusra Front</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">Islamic State</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Army_of_Conquest" title="Army of Conquest">Army of Conquest</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63"><span>[</span>63<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64"><span>[</span>64<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65"><span>[</span>65<span>]</span></a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/Russian_Air_Force" title="Russian Air Force">Russian Air Force</a> had significant ground support from the <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Armed_Forces" title="Syrian Armed Forces">Syrian military</a>, <a href="/wiki/Army_of_the_Guardians_of_the_Islamic_Revolution" title="Army of the Guardians of the Islamic Revolution">Iranian Revolutionary Guards</a>, and allied militias.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66"><span>[</span>66<span>]</span></a></sup> Prior to this intervention, <a href="/wiki/Russian_involvement_in_the_Syrian_Civil_War" title="Russian involvement in the Syrian Civil War">Russian involvement in the Syrian Civil War</a> had mainly consisted of supplying the <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Army" title="Syrian Army">Syrian Army</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67"><span>[</span>67<span>]</span></a></sup> Russia intervened after a formal request from the <a href="/wiki/Council_of_Ministers_(Syria)" title="Council of Ministers (Syria)">Syrian government</a> for military help against rebel and <a href="/wiki/Jihadist" title="Jihadist" class="mw-redirect">jihadist</a> groups in Syria.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68"><span>[</span>68<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p></p>

<p></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Background">Background</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Russian_military_intervention_in_the_Syrian_Civil_War&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Background">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote">See also: <a href="/wiki/Russian_involvement_in_the_Syrian_Civil_War" title="Russian involvement in the Syrian Civil War">Russian involvement in the Syrian Civil War</a></div>
<p>The Syrian Civil War is being waged between multiple opposition and government groups and their local and foreign support bases, who share a shifting, complex web of inter-relationships. As several months of air strikes conducted by the <a href="/wiki/Combined_Joint_Task_Force_%E2%80%93_Operation_Inherent_Resolve" title="Combined Joint Task Force – Operation Inherent Resolve">US-led coalition</a> ostensibly against <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq_and_the_Levant" title="Islamic State of Iraq and the Levant">ISIL</a> targets appeared to have resulted in further expansion and strengthening of the ISIL,<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69"><span>[</span>69<span>]</span></a></sup> Russia in September 2015 started sending its own Russian-operated warplanes and other military hardware as well as combat troops to an <a href="/wiki/Bassel_Al-Assad_International_Airport" title="Bassel Al-Assad International Airport">airbase</a> near the port city of <a href="/wiki/Latakia" title="Latakia">Latakia</a> in Syria.<sup id="cite_ref-buildup_70-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-buildup-70"><span>[</span>70<span>]</span></a></sup> The action was undertaken at an official request by the Syrian government headed by President <a href="/wiki/Bashar_al-Assad" title="Bashar al-Assad">Bashar al-Assad</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-auto_71-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-71"><span>[</span>71<span>]</span></a></sup> In October 2015, it was revealed<sup id="cite_ref-plot_72-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-plot-72"><span>[</span>72<span>]</span></a></sup> that the Russian operation in Syria may have been devised during the visit by <a href="/wiki/Qasem_Soleimani" title="Qasem Soleimani">Qasem Soleimani</a>, commander of the Iranian <a href="/wiki/Quds_Force" title="Quds Force">Quds Force</a>, to Moscow in July 2015, which was then denied by Russian officials.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73"><span>[</span>73<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74"><span>[</span>74<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>At the end of September 2015, a joint information centre in Baghdad was set up by Iran, Iraq, Russia and Syria to coordinate their operations against ISIL<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75"><span>[</span>75<span>]</span></a></sup> (in the newsmedia the centre is also referred to as "Joint Operations Room in Baghdad known as the 4 + 1" implying the Lebanese Shia militia <a href="/wiki/Hezbollah" title="Hezbollah">Hezbollah</a>, in addition to the 4 states<sup id="cite_ref-pedal_76-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-pedal-76"><span>[</span>76<span>]</span></a></sup>). According to Russian foreign minister <a href="/wiki/Sergey_Lavrov" title="Sergey Lavrov">Sergey Lavrov</a>′s statement made in mid-October 2015, prior to the start of its operations in Syria, Russia invited the U.S. to join the Baghdad-based information center but received what he called an "unconstructive" response; Putin′s proposal that the U.S. receive a high-level Russian delegation and that a U.S. delegation arrive in Moscow to discuss co-operation in Syria was likewise declined by the U.S.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77"><span>[</span>77<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78"><span>[</span>78<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79"><span>[</span>79<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>On 30 September 2015, the <a href="/wiki/Upper_house" title="Upper house">upper house</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Federal_Assembly_(Russia)" title="Federal Assembly (Russia)">Russian Federal Assembly</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Federation_Council_(Russia)" title="Federation Council (Russia)">Federation Council</a>, granted the request by Russian President <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Putin" title="Vladimir Putin">Vladimir Putin</a> to deploy the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Air_Force" title="Russian Air Force">Russian Air Force</a> in Syria.<sup id="cite_ref-gua_80-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-gua-80"><span>[</span>80<span>]</span></a></sup> On the same day, the Russian representative to the joint information centre arrived at the <a href="/wiki/Embassy_of_the_United_States,_Baghdad" title="Embassy of the United States, Baghdad">US Embassy in Baghdad</a> and requested that any U.S. forces in the targeted area in Syria leave immediately.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81"><span>[</span>81<span>]</span></a></sup> An hour later, the Russian aircraft based in the government-held territory began conducting airstrikes ostensibly against ISIL and other rebel targets.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82"><span>[</span>82<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Operations_by_Russian_military">Operations by Russian military</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Russian_military_intervention_in_the_Syrian_Civil_War&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Operations by Russian military">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote">See also: <a href="/wiki/2015_Russian_air_raids_in_Syria" title="2015 Russian air raids in Syria">2015 Russian air raids in Syria</a> and <a href="/wiki/Northwestern_Syria_offensive_(October_2015)" title="Northwestern Syria offensive (October 2015)">Northwestern Syria offensive (October 2015)</a></div>
<div class="thumb tleft">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Russian_military_aircraft_at_Latakia,_Syria_(1).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Russian_military_aircraft_at_Latakia%2C_Syria_%281%29.jpg/220px-Russian_military_aircraft_at_Latakia%2C_Syria_%281%29.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Russian_military_aircraft_at_Latakia%2C_Syria_%281%29.jpg/330px-Russian_military_aircraft_at_Latakia%2C_Syria_%281%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Russian_military_aircraft_at_Latakia%2C_Syria_%281%29.jpg/440px-Russian_military_aircraft_at_Latakia%2C_Syria_%281%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Russian_military_aircraft_at_Latakia,_Syria_(1).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Russian <a href="/wiki/Sukhoi_Su-24" title="Sukhoi Su-24">Su-24</a> jet aircraft at an air base in Latakia, Syria</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The first series of <a href="/wiki/Airstrike" title="Airstrike">air strikes</a> took place on 30 September 2015 in areas around the cities of <a href="/wiki/Homs" title="Homs">Homs</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hama" title="Hama">Hama</a>, targeting the <a href="/wiki/Syrian_opposition" title="Syrian opposition">mainstream opposition</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-latimes_62-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-latimes-62"><span>[</span>62<span>]</span></a></sup> Russian warplanes attacked rebel positions "in <a href="/wiki/Al-Rastan" title="Al-Rastan">al-Rastan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Talbiseh" title="Talbiseh">Talbiseh</a> and Zafaraniya in <a href="/wiki/Homs_Governorate" title="Homs Governorate">Homs province</a>; Al-Tilol al-Hmer in <a href="/wiki/Quneitra_Governorate" title="Quneitra Governorate">Quneitra province</a>; Aydoun, a village on the outskirts of the town of <a href="/wiki/Al-Salamiyah" title="Al-Salamiyah">Salamiya</a>; Deer Foul, between <a href="/wiki/Hama" title="Hama">Hama</a> and <a href="/wiki/Homs" title="Homs">Homs</a>; and the outskirts of <a href="/wiki/Al-Salamiyah" title="Al-Salamiyah">Salmiya</a>".<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83"><span>[</span>83<span>]</span></a></sup> In total, 20 flights were made.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84"><span>[</span>84<span>]</span></a></sup> Most of the initial airstrikes targeted positions of the <a href="/wiki/Foreign_rebel_fighters_in_the_Syrian_Civil_War#Chechnya_and_Russia" title="Foreign rebel fighters in the Syrian Civil War">Chechen fighters</a>, <a href="/wiki/Islamic_Front_(Syria)" title="Islamic Front (Syria)">Islamic Front</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Jaysh_al-Islam" title="Jaysh al-Islam">Jaysh al-Islam</a> (Army of Islam),<sup id="cite_ref-fisk_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-fisk-30"><span>[</span>30<span>]</span></a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Free_Syrian_Army" title="Free Syrian Army">Free Syrian Army</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85"><span>[</span>85<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86"><span>[</span>86<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87"><span>[</span>87<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>According to <a href="/wiki/Hezbollah" title="Hezbollah">Hezbollah</a> media outlet <a href="/wiki/Al_Mayadeen" title="Al Mayadeen">Al Mayadeen</a>, the Saudi/Turkish-backed <a href="/wiki/Army_of_Conquest" title="Army of Conquest">Army of Conquest</a><sup id="cite_ref-weekly_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-weekly-12"><span>[</span>12<span>]</span></a></sup> around Jisr ash-Shugour was bombed on 1 October by Russian planes; at least 30 air strikes were carried out.<sup id="cite_ref-vice1oct_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vice1oct-17"><span>[</span>17<span>]</span></a></sup> Another series of Russian airstrikes carried out that same day hit <a href="/wiki/ISIL" title="ISIL" class="mw-redirect">ISIL</a> positions in Raqqa governorate.<sup id="cite_ref-reuters1octraqqa_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-reuters1octraqqa-3"><span>[</span>3<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>On 2 October, head of the foreign-affairs committee in the <a href="/wiki/State_Duma" title="State Duma">Russian parliament</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aleksey_Pushkov" title="Aleksey Pushkov">Aleksey Pushkov</a>, said that the Russian airstrikes could go on for three to four months and would intensify;<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88"><span>[</span>88<span>]</span></a></sup> he later said that this was a mere surmise of his and he was not privy to any knowledge on the issue.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89"><span>[</span>89<span>]</span></a></sup> In the morning, the Russian Air Force launched four airstrikes on ISIL in the ancient <a href="/wiki/Assyrian_people" title="Assyrian people">Syriac</a> city of <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaryatayn" title="Al-Qaryatayn">Al-Qaryatayn</a>, and the T4-Palmyra highway, <a href="/wiki/Homs_Governorate" title="Homs Governorate">Homs province</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Oct_2_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Oct_2-26"><span>[</span>26<span>]</span></a></sup> An ISIL command and control center was destroyed in a single airstrike in Al-Qaryatayn, while an ISIL convoy on their way to the Teefor-Palmyra highway was attacked.<sup id="cite_ref-Oct_2_26-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Oct_2-26"><span>[</span>26<span>]</span></a></sup> Following the airstrikes, the <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Army" title="Syrian Army">Syrian Army</a> and <a href="/wiki/National_Defence_Forces_(Syria)" title="National Defence Forces (Syria)">National Defence Forces</a> pushed ISIL out of the town of Maheen towards Al-Qaryatayn after a two-hour engagement that killed 18 militants and destroyed two technicals mounted with <a href="/wiki/ZU-23-2" title="ZU-23-2">ZU-23-2s</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Oct_2_26-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Oct_2-26"><span>[</span>26<span>]</span></a></sup> Syrian forces then launched a counter-attack south-west of Al-Qaryatayn to recover the main road.<sup id="cite_ref-Oct_2_26-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Oct_2-26"><span>[</span>26<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>In the same day, the Russian Air Force began bombing <a href="/wiki/Al-Nusra_Front" title="Al-Nusra Front">Al-Nusra Front</a><sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90"><span>[</span>90<span>]</span></a></sup> positions in al-Rastan and Talbiseh in the <a href="/wiki/Homs_Governorate" title="Homs Governorate">Homs province</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-East_15-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-East-15"><span>[</span>15<span>]</span></a></sup> Later, they proceeded with bombing Al-Nusra in <a href="/wiki/Kafr_Zita" title="Kafr Zita">Kafr Zita</a>, Al-Ghaab Plains, <a href="/wiki/Kafr_Nabl" title="Kafr Nabl">Kafr Nabl</a>, Kafr Sijnah, and Al-Rakaya in the <a href="/wiki/Hama_Governorate" title="Hama Governorate">Hama province</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-East_15-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-East-15"><span>[</span>15<span>]</span></a></sup> The Syrian Air Force and the Russian Air Force jointly bombed Al-Nusra in <a href="/wiki/Jisr_al-Shughur" title="Jisr al-Shughur">Jisr al-Shughur</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-East_15-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-East-15"><span>[</span>15<span>]</span></a></sup> At night, the Russian Air Force targeted ISIL with 11 airstrikes over <a href="/wiki/Al-Raqqah" title="Al-Raqqah">Al-Raqqah</a> while targeting electrical grids outside it, two airstrikes over Shadadi-Hasakah highway, and three airstrikes in Al-Mayadeen, <a href="/wiki/Deir_ez-Zor_Governorate" title="Deir ez-Zor Governorate">Deir ez-Zor province</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-East_15-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-East-15"><span>[</span>15<span>]</span></a></sup> The primary ISIL military base in <a href="/wiki/Al-Thawrah" title="Al-Thawrah">Tabaqa</a> Military Airport was also attacked, with the barracks being destroyed in two airstrikes. Near the Military Airport, an ISIL weapons supply depot in Al-'Ajrawi Farms was also bombed. At the same time, the ISIL primary headquarters in Tabaqa National Hospital was heavily damaged in a Russian airstrike.<sup id="cite_ref-East_15-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-East-15"><span>[</span>15<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Tabaqa_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tabaqa-16"><span>[</span>16<span>]</span></a></sup> In <a href="/wiki/Al-Hasakah_Governorate" title="Al-Hasakah Governorate">Al-Hasakah province</a>, the Russian Air Force targeted ISIL in Al-Shadadi and Al-Houl, while the Syrian Air Force attacked an ISIL convoy along the Deir ez-Zor-Hasakah highway.<sup id="cite_ref-Tabaqa_16-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tabaqa-16"><span>[</span>16<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>On 3 October, reports indicated that Hezbollah and Iranian fighters were preparing major ground offensives to be coordinated with Russian airstrikes.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91"><span>[</span>91<span>]</span></a></sup> According to CNN, the Russian defense ministry said its soldiers bombed nine ISIL positions near the terror group's de facto capital in Raqqa. At least 11 were killed in an alleged double strike by Russia in Syria's Idlib province, according to opposition groups.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92"><span>[</span>92<span>]</span></a></sup> During the day, the Russian Air Force made four airstrikes over Al-Nusra controlled Jisr al-Shughur, and additional ones in <a href="/wiki/Zawiya_Mountain" title="Zawiya Mountain">Jabal Al-Zawiya</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Jabal_al-Akrad" title="Jabal al-Akrad">Jabal al-Akrad</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Oct_3_93-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Oct_3-93"><span>[</span>93<span>]</span></a></sup> One of the targets was an Al-Nusra reinforcement convoy heading from Jisr al-Shughur to the northeast countryside of <a href="/wiki/Latakia_Governorate" title="Latakia Governorate">Latakia province</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Oct_3_93-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Oct_3-93"><span>[</span>93<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>On the morning of 7 October 2015, according to the Russian officials, four warships from the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Navy" title="Russian Navy">Russian Navy</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Caspian_Flotilla" title="Caspian Flotilla">Caspian Flotilla</a> launched 26 <a href="/wiki/3M-54_Klub" title="3M-54 Klub">3M-14T Kalibr NK</a><sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94"><span>[</span>94<span>]</span></a></sup> cruise missiles that hit 11 targets within Syrian territory. The missiles passed through Iranian and Iraqi airspace in order to reach their targets at a distance of well over about 1,500 kilometers (930 miles).<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95"><span>[</span>95<span>]</span></a></sup> The same day, Syrian ground forces were reported to carry out an offensive under Russian air cover.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96"><span>[</span>96<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97"><span>[</span>97<span>]</span></a></sup> According to <a href="/wiki/CNN" title="CNN">CNN</a> citing unnamed U.S. military and intelligence officials, 4 of 26 cruise missiles on 8 October crashed in Iran, well before reaching their targets in Syria.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98"><span>[</span>98<span>]</span></a></sup> Russia claimed all of its missiles hit their targets.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99"><span>[</span>99<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100"><span>[</span>100<span>]</span></a></sup>Iran also denied any missile crash on its territory.<sup id="cite_ref-farsnews.com_101-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-farsnews.com-101"><span>[</span>101<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102"><span>[</span>102<span>]</span></a></sup> Iranian defence ministry rejected any reports alleging that four of the 26 cruise missiles crashed in Iran saying the CNN reports are part of the West's "psychological warfare".<sup id="cite_ref-farsnews.com_101-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-farsnews.com-101"><span>[</span>101<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>On 8 October 2015, the number of air raids increased significantly up to over 60 sorties a day, a tempo maintained for the next 2 days.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103"><span>[</span>103<span>]</span></a></sup> The Russian defense ministry announced on 9 October that up to sixty ISIL targets were hit in the past 24 hours, supposedly killing 300 militants in the most intense strikes so far. One of the raids targeted a <a href="/wiki/Liwa_al-Haqq_(Idlib,_Syria)" title="Liwa al-Haqq (Idlib, Syria)">Liwa al-Haqq</a> base in the <a href="/wiki/Al-Raqqah_Governorate" title="Al-Raqqah Governorate">Al-Raqqah Governorate</a> using <a href="/wiki/KAB-500KR" title="KAB-500KR">KAB-500KR</a> precision-guided bombs, in which two senior ISIL commanders and up to 200 militants were killed, despite the lack of connection between Liwa al-Haqq and ISIL. Another assault destroyed a former prison near Aleppo that was used by ISIL as a base and munitions depot, also killing scores of militants. Rebel training sites in the Latakia and Idlib provinces were allegedly hit as well.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104"><span>[</span>104<span>]</span></a></sup> Meanwhile, ISIL militants made advances in the Aleppo area on 9 October, seizing several villages, including Tal Qrah, Tal Sousin, and Kfar Qares, in what the <a href="/wiki/Associated_Press" title="Associated Press">Associated Press</a> called a "lightning attack". The attacks were unencumbered by either Russian or U.S.-led coalition airstrikes. The ISIL advance came at the expense of rebel groups also targeted by Russian and Syrian forces.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105"><span>[</span>105<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>On 13 October, the Russian military reported 88 sorties carried out in Syria in the previous 24 hours.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106"><span>[</span>106<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Iran.27s_involvement">Iran's involvement</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Russian_military_intervention_in_the_Syrian_Civil_War&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Iran's involvement">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote">See also: <a href="/wiki/Iranian_support_for_Syria_in_the_Syrian_Civil_War" title="Iranian support for Syria in the Syrian Civil War" class="mw-redirect">Iranian support for Syria in the Syrian Civil War</a></div>
<p>Iran continues to officially deny the presence of its combat troops in Syria, maintaining that it provides military advice to Assad's forces in their fight against terrorist groups.<sup id="cite_ref-denies_107-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-denies-107"><span>[</span>107<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>Key victories were achieved with substantial support provided by the Quds force, namely the al-Ghab plains battles, <a href="/wiki/Aleppo" title="Aleppo">Aleppo</a> offensives, Dara'aya offensives of 2015 and the al-Qusayr offensives which established government and Hezbollah control over the northern <a href="/wiki/Qalamoun" title="Qalamoun" class="mw-redirect">Qalamoun</a> region and the border crossings from Lebanon to Syria. In June 2015, some reports suggested that the Iranian military were effectively in charge of the Syrian government troops on the battlefield.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108"><span>[</span>108<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Idlib" title="Second Battle of Idlib">loss</a> of <a href="/wiki/Idlib_province" title="Idlib province" class="mw-redirect">Idlib province</a> to a <a href="/wiki/Northwestern_Syria_offensive_(April%E2%80%93June_2015)" title="Northwestern Syria offensive (April–June 2015)">rebel offensive</a> in the first half of 2015, the situation was judged to have become critical for Assad's survival. High level talks were held between Moscow and Tehran in the first half of 2015 and a political agreement was achieved;<sup id="cite_ref-plot_72-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-plot-72"><span>[</span>72<span>]</span></a></sup> on 24 July, ten days after the signing of the nuclear agreement between Iran and the P5+1 countries, general Qasem Soleimani visited Moscow<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109"><span>[</span>109<span>]</span></a></sup> to devise the details of the plan for coordinated military action in Syria.<sup id="cite_ref-plot_72-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-plot-72"><span>[</span>72<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110"><span>[</span>110<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>In mid-September 2015, the first reports of new detachments from the Iranian revolutionary guards arriving in <a href="/wiki/Tartus" title="Tartus">Tartus</a> and Latakia in west Syria were made. With much of the SAA and NDF units deployed to more volatile fronts, the Russian Marines and Iranian Revolutionary Guard (IRG) have relieved their positions by installing military checkpoints inside the cities of Slunfeh (east Latakia Governorate), <a href="/wiki/Masyaf" title="Masyaf">Masyaf</a> (East Tartus Governorate) and <a href="/wiki/Ras_al-Bassit" title="Ras al-Bassit">Ras al-Bassit</a> (Latakia coastal city).<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111"><span>[</span>111<span>]</span></a></sup> There were also further reports of new Iranian contingents being deployed to Syria in early October 2015.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112"><span>[</span>112<span>]</span></a></sup> It is generally thought that Iran will be playing a leading role in the ground operations of Syria's army and allies, whilst Russia will be leading in the air in conjunction with the Syrian air force, thereby establishing a complementary role.<sup id="cite_ref-theglobeandmail.com_19-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-theglobeandmail.com-19"><span>[</span>19<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>Outside of the battlefield itself the Iranian government has dramatically increased its efforts in supporting the Syrian government and its military. Recently there has been an exponential increase in recruitment efforts aimed at drawing on Shi'ite militias in Iraq in order to deploy them to Syria.<sup id="cite_ref-businessinsider.com_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-businessinsider.com-28"><span>[</span>28<span>]</span></a></sup> One of the leading militias in Iran's efforts to bolster the war effort in Syria is <a href="/wiki/Kata%27ib_al-Imam_Ali" title="Kata'ib al-Imam Ali">Kata'ib al-Imam Ali</a>, with Jaafar al-Bindawi, the militia's former head of training and logistics, would be leading the deployment in Syria, while Ali Nizam would serve as the new logistical director for Syrian affairs. Another important allied militia in this context is Harakat Hezbollah al-Nujaba which similar to Kata'ib al-Imam Ali was formed with Iranian assistance from mainly former Sadrist supporters and fighters. There is increasing evidence that these Iranian-backed militias are not only operating under Iranian guidance but are also cooperating with the Russian military command established in Syria.<sup id="cite_ref-businessinsider.com_28-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-businessinsider.com-28"><span>[</span>28<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>On 8 October 2015, reports came in of the death of brigadier general <a href="/wiki/Hossein_Hamadani" title="Hossein Hamadani">Hossein Hamadani</a>, the deputy to General <a href="/wiki/Qasem_Soleimani" title="Qasem Soleimani">Qasem Soleimani</a> in Syria;<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113"><span>[</span>113<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-leithfadel_27-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-leithfadel-27"><span>[</span>27<span>]</span></a></sup> his death was assessed by a U.S. intelligence officer as "a psychological blow to pro-regime forces in Syria".<sup id="cite_ref-assessed_114-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-assessed-114"><span>[</span>114<span>]</span></a></sup> On 12 October, two more senior commanders of the Iranian Revolutionary Guard Corps, Hamid Mokhtarband and Farshad Hassounizadeh, were reported by Iranian media to have been killed in Syria.<sup id="cite_ref-2more_56-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2more-56"><span>[</span>56<span>]</span></a></sup> The top-ranking losses notwithstanding, on 14 October preparations for the <a href="/wiki/Russian-Syrian-Iranian-Hezbollah_offensive" title="Russian-Syrian-Iranian-Hezbollah offensive">Russian-Syrian-Iranian-Hezbollah offensive</a> targeting rebels in Aleppo were said to continue apace.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115"><span>[</span>115<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116"><span>[</span>116<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117"><span>[</span>117<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>At least 121 IRGC troops, including several commanders, have been killed in the Syrian Civil War since it began.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118"><span>[</span>118<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119"><span>[</span>119<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120"><span>[</span>120<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Reactions">Reactions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Russian_military_intervention_in_the_Syrian_Civil_War&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Reactions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Involved_parties">Involved parties</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Russian_military_intervention_in_the_Syrian_Civil_War&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Involved parties">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Vladimir_Putin_and_Barack_Obama_(2015-09-29)_04.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Vladimir_Putin_and_Barack_Obama_%282015-09-29%29_04.jpg/220px-Vladimir_Putin_and_Barack_Obama_%282015-09-29%29_04.jpg" width="220" height="136" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Vladimir_Putin_and_Barack_Obama_%282015-09-29%29_04.jpg/330px-Vladimir_Putin_and_Barack_Obama_%282015-09-29%29_04.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Vladimir_Putin_and_Barack_Obama_%282015-09-29%29_04.jpg/440px-Vladimir_Putin_and_Barack_Obama_%282015-09-29%29_04.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1880" data-file-height="1160" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Vladimir_Putin_and_Barack_Obama_(2015-09-29)_04.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Russian and US representatives meet to discuss the situation in Syria on 29 September 2015</div>
</div>
</div>
<p><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Russia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Russia.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Russia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Russia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/f3/Flag_of_Russia.svg/45px-Flag_of_Russia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span>Russian Federation: On 1 October 2015, President Vladimir Putin dismissed unidentified media reports of alleged casualties among civilians caused by Russian airstrikes in Syria as "information warfare" against Russia, stating that the claims had begun before the planes used in the airstrikes had even taken off.<sup id="cite_ref-RT1Oct15_121-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RT1Oct15-121"><span>[</span>121<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>On 12 October 2015, Putin appealed to members of the <a href="/wiki/American-led_intervention_in_Syria" title="American-led intervention in Syria">American-led intervention in Syria</a> to join the Russian military intervention in the Syrian Civil War, highlighting the legality of Russia's intervention at Syria's request and questioning whether the U.S. one was valid at all. He highlighted the legitimate authority of Syria's fledgling <a href="/wiki/Constitutional_democracy" title="Constitutional democracy" class="mw-redirect">constitutional democracy</a> and lambasted the scrapped <a href="/wiki/Pentagon" title="Pentagon">Pentagon</a> program funding rebel training in Syria, saying "It would have been better to give us $500 million. At least we would have used it more effectively from the point of view of fighting international terrorism."<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122"><span>[</span>122<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>On 13 October 2015, Putin criticized the leaders of the American-led intervention in Syria as having mush for brains ("<a href="/wiki/Kasha" title="Kasha">kasha</a> in their heads"<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123"><span>[</span>123<span>]</span></a></sup>) for sending arms to the area that could end up in the wrong hands. He also criticized the American decision not to share with Russia information regarding potential ISIL targets.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124"><span>[</span>124<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>In mid-October 2015, Russian prime minister <a href="/wiki/Dmitry_Medvedev" title="Dmitry Medvedev">Dmitry Medvedev</a>, talking of the U.S. government′s refusal to engage in dialogue with Russia on cooperation in Syria, called this a "silly behavior": "As a result of these decisions and the cancellation of talks, the Americans have demonstrated their weakness." He added Russia remained open to discussion of "any issues".<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125"><span>[</span>125<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126"><span>[</span>126<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Flag_of_Syria.svg/23px-Flag_of_Syria.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Flag_of_Syria.svg/35px-Flag_of_Syria.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/53/Flag_of_Syria.svg/45px-Flag_of_Syria.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span>Syria: Ambassador to Russia, Riyad Haddad, stated that the Russian air force is acting in full coordination with the Syrian army. He added that Syria's position is that the Russian intervention is the only legitimate intervention under <a href="/wiki/International_law" title="International law">international law</a> and called for other countries to join the "non-criminal" Russian intervention in Syria.<sup id="cite_ref-auto_71-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-71"><span>[</span>71<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="International">International</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Russian_military_intervention_in_the_Syrian_Civil_War&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: International">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl>
<dt>Supranational</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Flag_of_NATO.svg/20px-Flag_of_NATO.svg.png" width="20" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Flag_of_NATO.svg/31px-Flag_of_NATO.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/37/Flag_of_NATO.svg/40px-Flag_of_NATO.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span>NATO - NATO has condemned Russian air strikes<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127"><span>[</span>127<span>]</span></a></sup> and urged Russia to stop supporting Syrian President Bashar al-Assad. On 8 October, they renewed assurances to defend the allies in view of the "escalation of Russian military activities."<sup id="cite_ref-nato_128-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-nato-128"><span>[</span>128<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>States</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Egypt.svg/23px-Flag_of_Egypt.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Egypt.svg/35px-Flag_of_Egypt.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Flag_of_Egypt.svg/45px-Flag_of_Egypt.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="900" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span>Egypt - On 3 October, Foreign Minister <a href="/wiki/Sameh_Shoukry" title="Sameh Shoukry">Sameh Shoukry</a> said the Russian entry into war in Syria was bound "to have an effect on limiting terrorism in Syria and eradicating it."<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129"><span>[</span>129<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Vladimir_Putin_and_Benyamin_Netanyahu_(22-09-2015)_02.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Vladimir_Putin_and_Benyamin_Netanyahu_%2822-09-2015%29_02.jpg/220px-Vladimir_Putin_and_Benyamin_Netanyahu_%2822-09-2015%29_02.jpg" width="220" height="136" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Vladimir_Putin_and_Benyamin_Netanyahu_%2822-09-2015%29_02.jpg/330px-Vladimir_Putin_and_Benyamin_Netanyahu_%2822-09-2015%29_02.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Vladimir_Putin_and_Benyamin_Netanyahu_%2822-09-2015%29_02.jpg/440px-Vladimir_Putin_and_Benyamin_Netanyahu_%2822-09-2015%29_02.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1880" data-file-height="1160" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Vladimir_Putin_and_Benyamin_Netanyahu_(22-09-2015)_02.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu" title="Benjamin Netanyahu">Benjamin Netanyahu</a> meets with <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Putin" title="Vladimir Putin">Vladimir Putin</a> in Moscow, 21 September 2015</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/21px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png" width="21" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/32px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d4/Flag_of_Israel.svg/41px-Flag_of_Israel.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="660" data-file-height="480" />&#160;</span>Israel - Shortly prior to the Russian intervention, the <a href="/wiki/Israel_Defense_Forces" title="Israel Defense Forces">Israel Defense Forces</a> and Russian military had set up a joint working group to coordinate their Syria-related activities in the aerial, naval, and electromagnetic arenas.<sup id="cite_ref-workinggroup_130-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-workinggroup-130"><span>[</span>130<span>]</span></a></sup> The Israeli government was primarily concerned about ensuring that the potential alliance between <a href="/wiki/Hezbollah" title="Hezbollah">Hezbollah</a> and Russia is not detrimental to its security.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131"><span>[</span>131<span>]</span></a></sup> According to <a href="/wiki/Zvi_Magen" title="Zvi Magen">Zvi Magen</a>, former ambassador to Moscow, "Israel made clear to him [Putin] that we have no real problem with Assad, just with Iran and Hezbollah, and that message was understood."<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132"><span>[</span>132<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Flag_of_Saudi_Arabia.svg/23px-Flag_of_Saudi_Arabia.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Flag_of_Saudi_Arabia.svg/35px-Flag_of_Saudi_Arabia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Flag_of_Saudi_Arabia.svg/45px-Flag_of_Saudi_Arabia.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="750" data-file-height="500" />&#160;</span>Saudi Arabia - On 1 October, Saudi Arabia′s senior diplomat at the UN demanded that Russia cease its intervention, repeating claims made by Western diplomats that Russia was targeting the unnamed "moderate" anti-government opposition rather than ISIL.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133"><span>[</span>133<span>]</span></a></sup>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Erdo%C4%9Fan_and_Putin.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Erdo%C4%9Fan_and_Putin.jpg/220px-Erdo%C4%9Fan_and_Putin.jpg" width="220" height="136" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Erdo%C4%9Fan_and_Putin.jpg/330px-Erdo%C4%9Fan_and_Putin.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f7/Erdo%C4%9Fan_and_Putin.jpg/440px-Erdo%C4%9Fan_and_Putin.jpg 2x" data-file-width="940" data-file-height="580" /></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Erdo%C4%9Fan_and_Putin.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Erdoğan visited Moscow to discuss Syria and to attend the opening of the newly built <a href="/wiki/Moscow_Cathedral_Mosque" title="Moscow Cathedral Mosque">Cathedral Mosque</a>, 23 September 2015</div>
</div>
</div>
</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Flag_of_Turkey.svg/23px-Flag_of_Turkey.svg.png" width="23" height="15" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Flag_of_Turkey.svg/35px-Flag_of_Turkey.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b4/Flag_of_Turkey.svg/45px-Flag_of_Turkey.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="800" />&#160;</span>Turkey - President <a href="/wiki/Recep_Tayyip_Erdo%C4%9Fan" title="Recep Tayyip Erdoğan">Recep Tayyip Erdoğan</a>, after a series of violations of the country′s airspace by Russian military aircraft in early October, warned that Russia's military operation in Syria could <a href="/wiki/Russia-Turkey_relations" title="Russia-Turkey relations" class="mw-redirect">jeopardise the bilateral ties between the countries</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134"><span>[</span>134<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/ae/Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" />&#160;</span>United Kingdom - Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/David_Cameron" title="David Cameron">David Cameron</a> said "It's absolutely clear that Russia is not discriminating between Isil [IS] and the legitimate Syrian opposition groups and, as a result, they are actually backing the butcher Assad and helping him".<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135"><span>[</span>135<span>]</span></a></sup> British troops will be sent to the <a href="/wiki/Baltic_states" title="Baltic states">Baltic states</a> and Poland following Russia's intervention in Syria "to respond to any further provocation and aggression".<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136"><span>[</span>136<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1235" data-file-height="650" />&#160;</span>USA - In early October, President <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> was reported to have authorised the resupply—against ISIL—of 25,000 Syrian Kurds and 5,000 of the armed-<a href="/wiki/Syrian_opposition" title="Syrian opposition">Syrian opposition</a>, emphasising that the U.S. would continue this support now that Russia had joined the conflict.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137"><span>[</span>137<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-cnn_138-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cnn-138"><span>[</span>138<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>The U.S. ruled out military cooperation with Russia in Syria.<sup id="cite_ref-carter_139-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-carter-139"><span>[</span>139<span>]</span></a></sup> Secretary of Defense <a href="/wiki/Ashton_Carter" title="Ashton Carter" class="mw-redirect">Ashton Carter</a> and other senior U.S. officials said Russia's campaign was primarily aimed at propping up Assad, whom President <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> has repeatedly called upon to leave power,<sup id="cite_ref-auto2_140-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto2-140"><span>[</span>140<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
<dd>On 8 October, U.S. Defense Secretary <a href="/wiki/Ashton_Carter" title="Ashton Carter" class="mw-redirect">Ashton Carter</a>, talking at a meeting of NATO defence ministers in Brussels, said he believed Russia would soon start paying the price for its military intervention in Syria in the form of reprisal attacks and casualties.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141"><span>[</span>141<span>]</span></a></sup> He added that he expected "in the next few days the Russians will begin to lose in Syria."<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142"><span>[</span>142<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-carter_139-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-carter-139"><span>[</span>139<span>]</span></a></sup> He further said Russia's campaign was primarily aimed at propping up Assad,<sup id="cite_ref-auto2_140-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto2-140"><span>[</span>140<span>]</span></a></sup></dd>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Flag_of_Cuba.svg/23px-Flag_of_Cuba.svg.png" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Flag_of_Cuba.svg/35px-Flag_of_Cuba.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Flag_of_Cuba.svg/46px-Flag_of_Cuba.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="800" data-file-height="400" />&#160;</span>Cuba - Cuba has said claims it sent troops to fight in Syria were false.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143"><span>[</span>143<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144"><span>[</span>144<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145"><span>[</span>145<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146"><span>[</span>146<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>Joint statement</dt>
</dl>
<p><a href="/wiki/Military_intervention_against_ISIL#3_December_coalition" title="Military intervention against ISIL">U.S.-led coalition</a> - On 1 October, participants in the <a href="/wiki/Military_intervention_against_ISIL#3_December_coalition" title="Military intervention against ISIL">U.S.-led anti-ISIL coalition</a> called on Russia to curtail its air campaign in Syria, saying the airstrikes had hit Syrian opposition groups and civilians. Such strikes would "only fuel more extremism", the statement issued by the U.S., UK, Turkey and other coalition members declared.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147"><span>[</span>147<span>]</span></a></sup> "We call on the Russian Federation to immediately cease its attacks on the Syrian opposition and civilians and to focus its efforts on fighting ISIL."<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148"><span>[</span>148<span>]</span></a></sup> U.S. President Barack Obama, at a news conference on 2 October, underscored the coalition statement by saying the Russian action was driving moderate opposition groups underground, and would result in "only strengthening" IS.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149"><span>[</span>149<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Non-state">Non-state</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Russian_military_intervention_in_the_Syrian_Civil_War&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Non-state">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>Representatives of the <a href="/wiki/Kurds_in_Syria" title="Kurds in Syria">Kurdish</a> <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Protection_Units" title="People's Protection Units">YPG</a> and <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Union_Party_(Syria)" title="Democratic Union Party (Syria)">PYD</a> expressed their support for Russian air strikes against Islamic State, al-Nusra Front and <a href="/wiki/Ahrar_ash-Sham" title="Ahrar ash-Sham">Ahrar ash-Sham</a>. They also asked for Russian help in weaponry and for the cooperation with Russia in the fight against Islamic State.<sup id="cite_ref-al-monitor_150-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-al-monitor-150"><span>[</span>150<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151"><span>[</span>151<span>]</span></a></sup> Shortly after the Russian air strikes started, <a href="/wiki/Salih_Muslim" title="Salih Muslim" class="mw-redirect">Salih Muslim</a>, co-chair of the PYD, has said in an interview that he doesn't believe "that America will object because [Jabhat] al-Nusra and Ahrar al-Sham are no different than Daesh. They are all terrorist organizations and share the same radical mentality."<sup id="cite_ref-al-monitor_150-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-al-monitor-150"><span>[</span>150<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>On 30 September, <a href="/wiki/Russian_Orthodox_Church" title="Russian Orthodox Church">Russian Orthodox Church</a> spokesman <a href="/wiki/Vsevolod_Chaplin" title="Vsevolod Chaplin">Vsevolod Chaplin</a>, talking about the support of the government's action on the part of all the religious groups in Russia, said the fight against terrorism was a "moral fight, a <a href="/wiki/Religious_war" title="Religious war">holy fight</a> if you will".<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152"><span>[</span>152<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153"><span>[</span>153<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154"><span>[</span>154<span>]</span></a></sup> Leader of the Central Spiritual Administration of <a href="/wiki/Islam_in_Russia" title="Islam in Russia">Muslims of Russia</a>, Chief Mufti <a href="/wiki/Talgat_Tadzhuddin" title="Talgat Tadzhuddin">Talgat Tadzhuddin</a> stated: "We fully back the use of a contingent of Russian armed forces in the battle against international terrorism."<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155"><span>[</span>155<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>Over 40 anti-government groups, including factions such as <a href="/wiki/Ahrar_ash-Sham" title="Ahrar ash-Sham">Ahrar ash-Sham</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jaysh_al-Islam" title="Jaysh al-Islam">Jaysh al-Islam</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Levant_Front" title="Levant Front">Levant Front</a>, were reported, on 5 October, to have vowed to attack Russian forces in retaliation for Moscow's air campaign.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156"><span>[</span>156<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda" title="Al-Qaeda">Al-Qaeda</a>'s Syrian affiliate <a href="/wiki/Al-Nusra_Front" title="Al-Nusra Front">al-Nusra Front</a><sup id="cite_ref-auto1_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto1-13"><span>[</span>13<span>]</span></a></sup> has set a reward for the seizure of Russian soldiers of 2,500,000 <a href="/wiki/Syrian_pound" title="Syrian pound">Syrian pounds</a> (approximately US$13,000).<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157"><span>[</span>157<span>]</span></a></sup> Abu Ubaid Al-Madani, who speaks Russian, released a video addressed to the Russians warning that they would massacre Russian soldiers and that "Your sons will return dead, are those Russian soldiers willing to die for the caprices and egoism of Putin?"<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158"><span>[</span>158<span>]</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Abu_Mohammad_al-Julani" title="Abu Mohammad al-Julani">Abu Mohammad al-Julani</a> called for Russian civilians to be attacked by former Soviet Muslims and called for attacks on <a href="/wiki/Alawites" title="Alawites">Alawite</a> villages in Syria.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159"><span>[</span>159<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160"><span>[</span>160<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161"><span>[</span>161<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>The Syria-based, Al-Qaeda linked Saudi cleric Abdallah Muhammad Al-Muhaysini threatened that Syria would be a "tomb for its invaders" or "graveyard for invaders" in response to the Russian intervention and brought up the Soviet war in Afghanistan.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162"><span>[</span>162<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163"><span>[</span>163<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164"><span>[</span>164<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Muslim_Brotherhood_of_Syria" title="Muslim Brotherhood of Syria">Muslim Brotherhood of Syria</a> issued a statement declaring <a href="/wiki/Jihad" title="Jihad">Jihad</a> against Russia obligatory (<a href="/wiki/Fard" title="Fard">Fard</a> 'ayn) upon all who are able to carry weapons.<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165"><span>[</span>165<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166"><span>[</span>166<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167"><span>[</span>167<span>]</span></a></sup> They cited the Russian Orthodox Church's call of the operation as a Holy War.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168"><span>[</span>168<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169"><span>[</span>169<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170"><span>[</span>170<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171"><span>[</span>171<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172"><span>[</span>172<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173"><span>[</span>173<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174"><span>[</span>174<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>Fifty-five Saudi religious scholars signed a statement against the Russian intervention, first addressing the Russians as "Oh Russians, oh extremist people of the Cross", reminding them of the Soviet invasion of Afghanistan and addressing the Orthodox Russia as the heir of the Soviet Communists, accusing them of "supporting the Nusayri regime" and invading "Muslim Syria", accusing the leaders of the Russian Orthodox Church of declaring a "Crusade" and telling them they will meet the fate of the Soviet Union and suffer "a shameful defeat in the Levant" as what happened in Afghanistan. The statement also addressed "Our people in the Levant", telling able-bodied and people who are able to contribute to join the "Jihad" instead of emigrating. The statement also called for all factions against the government in Syria to unite; the statement addressed "Arab and Muslim countries", telling them that there is a "real war against Sunnis and their countries and identity" at the hands of the "Western-Russian and Safavid and Nusayri alliance", calling for the termination of all relations with Iran and Russia with Muslim countries and to "protect the land and people of the Levant from the influence of the Persians and Russians", especially calling upon Qatar, Turkey, and Saudi Arabia to support the Levant.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175"><span>[</span>175<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176"><span>[</span>176<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-177" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-177"><span>[</span>177<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178"><span>[</span>178<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179"><span>[</span>179<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180"><span>[</span>180<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181"><span>[</span>181<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-182" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-182"><span>[</span>182<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183"><span>[</span>183<span>]</span></a></sup> The statement called on "all those who are able, and outside of Saudi Arabia, to answer the calls of jihad".<sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184"><span>[</span>184<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185"><span>[</span>185<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Free_Syrian_Army" title="Free Syrian Army">Free Syrian Army</a>'s "Homs Liberation Movement" threatened <a href="/wiki/Suicide_attack" title="Suicide attack">suicide bombings</a> against Russians in Syria.<sup id="cite_ref-186" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-186"><span>[</span>186<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
<li>Photos of <a href="/wiki/Uyghur" title="Uyghur" class="mw-disambig">Uyghur</a> fighters of the <a href="/wiki/Turkistan_Islamic_Party" title="Turkistan Islamic Party" class="mw-redirect">Turkistan Islamic Party</a> were released with captions in Arabic that said "standing up strongly to the Nusayri army and the Russians." (المجاهدين التركستانيين يتصدى بقوة للجيش النصيري ومن قبل الروس).<sup id="cite_ref-187" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-187"><span>[</span>187<span>]</span></a></sup></li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Analysis_and_media">Analysis and media</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Russian_military_intervention_in_the_Syrian_Civil_War&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Analysis and media">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Prior to the start of the Russian operation in Syria as well as afterwards, Russian analysts believed that Russia′s military build-up in Syria was aimed <i>inter alia</i> at ending the <i>de facto</i> political and diplomatic isolation that the West had imposed on Putin in connection with the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Russian_military_intervention_in_Ukraine" title="2014–15 Russian military intervention in Ukraine">situation in Ukraine</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188"><span>[</span>188<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189"><span>[</span>189<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-190" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-190"><span>[</span>190<span>]</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191"><span>[</span>191<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>On 30 September, dozens of videos emerged in not specified “media” allegedly showing the effects of Russian bombings of residential areas causing civilian casualties.<sup id="cite_ref-RT1Oct15_121-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RT1Oct15-121"><span>[</span>121<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Thomas_L._Friedman" title="Thomas L. Friedman" class="mw-redirect">Thomas L. Friedman</a>, a columnist for the <i><a href="/wiki/New_York_Times" title="New York Times" class="mw-redirect">New York Times</a></i>, on 30 September, wrote that by allying himself with Syria and Iran in battle, Putin would "alienate the entire <a href="/wiki/Sunni_Muslim" title="Sunni Muslim" class="mw-redirect">Sunni Muslim</a> world, including Russian Muslims"; his advice to the Obama administration was: "Putin stupidly went into Syria looking for a cheap sugar high to show his people that Russia is still a world power. Well, now he’s up a tree. Obama and <a href="/wiki/John_Kerry" title="John Kerry">John Kerry</a> should just leave him up there for a month – him and Assad, fighting ISIS alone – and watch him become public enemy No. 1 in the Sunni Muslim world."<sup id="cite_ref-192" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-192"><span>[</span>192<span>]</span></a></sup> The publication <a href="/wiki/Voice_of_America" title="Voice of America">Voice of America</a> predicted a major backlash against the Russians at the hands of jihadists.<sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193"><span>[</span>193<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Jeremy_Shapiro" title="Jeremy Shapiro">Jeremy Shapiro</a>, a senior fellow in the <a href="/wiki/Brookings_Institution" title="Brookings Institution">Brookings Institution</a>, believed Putin′s military intervention was "incredibly stupid stuff" that had surprised the U.S., as they "had not understood that the Russians were this self-destructive."<sup id="cite_ref-stupid_194-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-stupid-194"><span>[</span>194<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p><a href="/wiki/Robert_Fisk" title="Robert Fisk">Robert Fisk</a>, senior Middle East correspondent for the <i><a href="/wiki/The_Independent" title="The Independent">The Independent</a></i>, wrote that "the Russian air force in Syria has flown straight into the West's fantasy air space. The Russians, we are now informed, are bombing the "moderates" in Syria – "moderates" whom even the Americans admitted two months ago, no longer existed."<sup id="cite_ref-fisk_30-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-fisk-30"><span>[</span>30<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Syrian_Arab_News_Agency" title="Syrian Arab News Agency">Syrian Arab News Agency</a> reported that anti-government fighters were in panic and fleeing Syria in their thousands in response to the Russian intervention. They expressed the view that the "moderate opposition" were in fact hired <a href="/wiki/Mercenaries" title="Mercenaries" class="mw-redirect">mercenaries</a> trained in <a href="/wiki/CIA" title="CIA" class="mw-redirect">CIA</a> supervised training camps in Turkey, Jordan, Qatar and Saudi Arabia, many of whom had switched allegiance and taken their weaponry to ISIL and other terrorist groups paying more once they controlled the <a href="/wiki/Oil_field" title="Oil field">oil fields</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195"><span>[</span>195<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>On 8 October 2015, the <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> quoted US-based analyst Michael Kofman as opining that Russia sought the defeat of fighters backed by the US, and its coalition allies, leaving the Islamic State and al-Nusra Front as the only alternatives to President Assad; he noted that a more robust American campaign against ISIL would be complementary to Russian goals, and a win-win scenario for Assad: "Ultimately, Russia and Iran have secured their position in Syria. Assad or no Assad, the West will have to deal with Russia directly, and most likely as an equal, in settlement to the Syrian conflict."<sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196"><span>[</span>196<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
<p>In mid-October 2015, <i><a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">The New York Times</a></i> opined that with anti-government insurgents in Syria receiving for the first time bountiful supplies of U.S.-made antitank missiles and with Russia raising the number of airstrikes against the government's opponents that had raised morale in both camps, broadening war objectives and hardening political positions, the conflict was turning into an all-out <a href="/wiki/Proxy_war" title="Proxy war">proxy war</a> between the U.S. and Russia.<sup id="cite_ref-larger_197-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-larger-197"><span>[</span>197<span>]</span></a></sup></p>
